        (function(d){
            var js, id = 'facebook-jssdk'; if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
            js = d.createElement('script'); js.id = id; js.async = true;
            js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js";
            d.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(js);
        }(document));

        document.observe('click', function(e){
            var target = e.findElement('*[rel^=facebook-connect]');

            if (target && target.readAttribute('rel')=='facebook-connect') {
                e.stop();
                try{
                    FB.login(function(response){
                        if(response.status=='connected') setLocation(fbRedirect);
                    }, {scope: "email"});
                }catch(error){}
            }

        });

        function MoveCustomBackground(){
            // Fix bug in paysafecard-exclusive-sale page
            if ( jQuery('.cms-paysafecard-exclusive-sale').length && !jQuery('.cms-paysafecard-exclusive-sale #top-banner').is(':visible') ) {
                jQuery('body > div.custom-background').css('margin-top', '0');
                return; // stop/end MoveCustomBackground
            }

            if (jQuery('body > div.custom-background').length) {
                var current_margin_top = jQuery('body > div.custom-background').css("margin-top").replace("px", "");
                var top_baner_height = jQuery('#top-banner').css('height').replace("px", "");
                var margin_top_after_top_baner_closed = current_margin_top - top_baner_height;

                jQuery('body > div.custom-background').css('margin-top', margin_top_after_top_baner_closed);
            }

<script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(document).ready(function() {

        jQuery(document).on("click", "#js-currency-switcher-toggle-button", function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            jQuery("#js-currency-switcher-currency_menu").toggle();
            jQuery("#js-currency-switcher-toggle-button").toggleClass("open");
        });

        jQuery(document).on("mouseup", "#js-currency-switcher-currency_menu", function() {
            return false;
        });

        jQuery(document).mouseup(function(e) {
            if(jQuery(e.target).parents("#js-currency-switcher").length==0) {
                jQuery("#js-currency-switcher-toggle-button").removeClass("open");
                jQuery("#js-currency-switcher-currency_menu").hide();
            }
        });
    });
</script>

                        callback: function(element, defaultUrl) {

    <script>

        jQuery(function() {
            jQuery('#cat_platform').ddslick();

            var search_padding = 'padding-left';
            var globalSearchInputWrapper = jQuery('#js-global__search-input-wrapper');
            
            if(jQuery('html').attr('lang') == 'ar'){
                search_padding = 'padding-right';
            }
            var cat_platform_width = jQuery("#cat_platform").width();
            var container_form_search = jQuery('.header #search_mini_form .form-search').width();
            jQuery('.header .form-search input.input-text').css(search_padding, cat_platform_width);
            var search = container_form_search - cat_platform_width - 50;
            jQuery('.header .form-search input.input-text').css('width', search );

            if( typeof  globalSearchInputWrapper != 'undefined' && globalSearchInputWrapper.length ) {
                globalSearchInputWrapper.css('width', search);
            }

            jQuery('#cat_platform').on('click', 'li', function () {
                var ddData = jQuery('#cat_platform').data('ddslick');

                var cat_platform_width = jQuery("#cat_platform").width();
                jQuery('.header .form-search input.input-text').css(search_padding, cat_platform_width);
                var search = container_form_search - cat_platform_width - 50;
                jQuery('.header .form-search input.input-text').css('width', search );

                if (ddData.selectedIndex < 1) {
                    var action = "https://www.kinguin.net/catalogsearch/result/index/";
                } else {
                    var action = "https://www.kinguin.net/catalogsearch/result/index/" + "platform_id/" +
                        ddData.selectedData.value;
                }
                jQuery("#search_mini_form").attr("action", action);
                //empty fake event
                searchForm.refresh();
            });

            jQuery('#search').on('focus', function () {
                if (jQuery('#search_autocomplete').css("display") == 'none' && jQuery('#search_autocomplete ul').children()
                    .size() > 0) {
                    jQuery('#search_autocomplete').show();
                }
            })
            /*
             jQuery('#show-more-search').on('click', function (e) {
             console.log('hi');
             e.preventDefault();
             })
             */
            jQuery('#search_autocomplete').on('click','li.ajax-result-item', function (e) {

               url = jQuery(this).find('.ajax-result a').attr('href');
               window.location = url;
               e.preventDefault();

            })

            jQuery('#search_autocomplete').on('click','#show-more-search', function (e) {
                jQuery('#search_mini_form').submit();
                e.preventDefault();
            })

            //jQuery(window).load(function() {
                jQuery('#cat_platform, #search').css('visibility','visible');
            //});

        });

    </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
        //<![CDATA[
        jQuery('.fdbk-comments').hover(function(){
            var title = jQuery(this).attr('title');
            if (title.length > 80) {
                jQuery(this).data('tipText', title).removeAttr('title');
                jQuery('<p class="tooltip-comments"></p>')
                    .text(title)
                    .appendTo('body')
                    .fadeIn('slow'); }
        }, function() {
            // Hover out code
            jQuery(this).attr('title', jQuery(this).data('tipText'));
            jQuery('.tooltip-comments').remove();
        }).mousemove(function(e) {
            var mousex = e.pageX + 20;
            var mousey = e.pageY + 10;
            jQuery('.tooltip-comments')
                .css({ top: mousey, left: mousex })
        });

        jQuery('.moment-timeago').each(function(i, el){
            var val = jQuery(el).text();
            val = moment(val, "YYYY-MM-DDHH:mm:ss").fromNow();

            jQuery(el).text(val);
        });
        //]]>
    </script>

<script>
    function displayMessage(elem1, elem2, display_time){
        elem1.fadeOut(600);
        elem2.fadeIn(600);
        setTimeout(function(){
            elem1.fadeIn(600);
            elem2.fadeOut(600);
        }, display_time);
    } 

    jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter form').submit(function(event){
        event.preventDefault();
        var userEmail = jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter input.subscription-email').val();
        var regex = /^([a-zA-Z0-9_.+-])+\@([a-zA-Z0-9_.+-])+$/;
        if(regex.test(userEmail)){
            jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter button[type="submit"]').attr('disabled', 'disabled').addClass('disabled');
            jQuery.post(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter form').attr('action'), { email: userEmail }, function(data){
                if(data.status){
                    switch(data.status){
                        case "success":
                            displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.success'), 5000);
                            jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter input.subscription-email').val('');
                            fbq('track', 'Lead');
                            newsletter_subscription_tracking_event();
                            break;

                        case "queued":
                            displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.queued'), 5000);
                            break;

                        case "added":
                            displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.added'), 5000);
                            break;

                        case "error":
                            displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.error'), 5000);
                            break;
                        case "incorrect":
                            displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.incorrect'), 2000);
                            break;
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.error'), 5000);
                }
            }.bind(this))
                .complete(function(xhr, status){
                     jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter button[type="submit"]').removeAttr('disabled').removeClass('disabled');
                    });
        }
        else{
            // incorect email
            displayMessage(jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.form'), jQuery('#subscribe-newsletter .newsletter-content.incorrect'), 2000);
        }
    });
</script>        <div id="footer-payment-methods">

<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function() {
    taxRate = parseFloat('1');
    addTaxes(taxRate, false, '.price.add-tax-rate');
});

function addTaxes(taxRate, forceCalculation, elements) {
    if (taxRate > 1 || forceCalculation) {
        var zeroPrecision = '0';
        var buyerProtectionSub = '0';
        var includeTaxPriceComparision = '0';
        var JSONpriceFormat =  '{"pattern":"$%s","precision":2,"requiredPrecision":2,"decimalSymbol":".","groupSymbol":",","groupLength":3,"integerRequired":1}';
        var priceFormat = JSONpriceFormat.evalJSON(true);
        var separator = priceFormat.decimalSymbol;
        jQuery(elements).each(function(e) {
            noTaxPrice = parseFloat(jQuery(this).attr('data-no-tax-price'));
            bpSubVal = 0;
            if (buyerProtectionSub == 1 && jQuery(this).next('.bp-sub').length) {
                bpSubVal = parseFloat(jQuery(this).next('.bp-sub').val());
            }

            if (bpSubVal > 0) {
                noTaxPrice = noTaxPrice - bpSubVal;
            }

            if (0 == includeTaxPriceComparision && jQuery(this).parent().hasClass('external-vendor-price')) {
                // don't add tax to price comparision offers
                priceWithTax = noTaxPrice;
            } else {
                priceWithTax = noTaxPrice * taxRate;
            }

            if (bpSubVal > 0) {
                priceWithTax = priceWithTax + bpSubVal;
            }

            priceWithTax = Math.round(priceWithTax * 1000) / 1000;
            priceWithTax = Math.round(priceWithTax * 100) / 100;
            if (zeroPrecision == 1) {
                priceWithTax = Math.round(Math.round(priceWithTax * 10) / 10);
            }

            priceWithTax = formatCurrency(priceWithTax, priceFormat);
            if (zeroPrecision == 1) {
                priceWithTax = priceWithTax.replace(separator+'00', '');

            }

            priceWithTaxElement = (priceWithTax + "").split(separator);
            priceLeft = priceWithTaxElement[0];
            if (priceLeft === undefined) {
                priceLeft = "";
            }

            priceRight = priceWithTaxElement[1];
            if (priceRight === undefined) {
                priceRight = "";
            } else {
                priceRight = separator + priceRight;
            }
            if (zeroPrecision == 1) {
                priceText = priceLeft;
            } else {
                priceText = priceLeft + '<span class="super">' + priceRight + '</span>';
            }

            if (taxRate == 1) {
                taxTxt = '';
            } else {
                taxTxt = '';      /*   text remove Incl. Tax  */
            }

            priceText += '<span class="tax-info">' + taxTxt + '</span>';

            jQuery(this).html(priceText);
        });
        
        percentElements = jQuery('.percent-price');
        if (percentElements.size() > 0) {
            jQuery(percentElements).each(function(e) {
                firstPrice = parseFloat(jQuery(this).attr('data-first-price'));
                secondPrice = parseFloat(jQuery(this).attr('data-second-price')) * taxRate;
                percent = parseInt((secondPrice / firstPrice) * 100 - 100);
                jQuery(this).html('<span>' + percent + '%</span>')
            })
            
        } 

                
        
        
    }
    jQuery('.price.add-tax-rate').removeClass('hidden');
}

    <script>
        (function () {

            function updateLivechatData() {
                var liveChatElements = $$('div[data-id="ba7f70bcda"]');

                if (liveChatElements.length==0) {
                    return false;
                }

                liveChatElements.each(function (elem) {
                    var liveChatElement = $(elem);

                    var liveChatImage = liveChatElement.up()
                        .down('.livechat_image');

                    if (!liveChatImage) {
                        var liveChatImage = liveChatElement.up('table.chat')
                            .down('.livechat_image');
                    }

                    var anchor = liveChatElement.down('a');
                    var anchorStatusElement = anchor.down('span.status');
                    var liveChatLoaded = false;
                    var anchorStatusValue = null;

                    if (anchorStatusElement) {
                        anchorStatusValue = anchorStatusElement.innerHTML
                            .replace('(' , '')
                            .replace(')' , '');
                    }

                    if (anchorStatusValue
                        && (anchorStatusValue=='online' || anchorStatusValue=='offline')) {

                        window.clearInterval(liveChatUpdateInterval);

                        liveChatElement.removeClassName('livechat-offline')
                            .addClassName('livechat-' + anchorStatusValue);

                        if (anchorStatusValue=='offline') {
                            anchor.writeAttribute('onclick', 'return false;');
                            anchor.innerHTML = '<span class="lc-label">Live Chat</span> <span class="status">(offline)</span>';

                            if (liveChatImage) {
                                liveChatImage.addClassName('livechat-offline');
                            }
                        } else if (anchorStatusValue=='online') {
                            anchor.innerHTML = '<span class="lc-label">Live Chat</span> <span class="status">(online)</span>';

                            $$('.livechat-offline-api').each(function (elem) {
                                $(elem).removeClassName('livechat-offline-api')
                                    .addClassName('livechat-online-api')
                            });

                            if (liveChatImage) {
                                liveChatImage.writeAttribute('onclick', anchor.readAttribute('onclick'));
                            }
                        }

                        return true;
                    }
                });

                return false;
            }

            window.liveChatUpdateInterval = setInterval(updateLivechatData, 1000);

            document.observe('click', function (e) {
                if (e.findElement('.livechat-offline')) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var targetElement = $(e.target);

                    // CONTACT US - PAYMENT METHOD FIX
                    if (targetElement.up('div.payment-popup-desc')) {
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (window.APP_VARS.can_go_to_contact_us) {
                        window.location = 'https://www.kinguin.net/contact-us/';
                    } else {
                        window.location = 'https://www.kinguin.net/helpdeskultimate/customer/newticket/';
                    }
                }
            });

        })();
    </script>
